#####

Old Phone will be rejected during pickup if

*   * Phone is not in working condition
  * RAM/Storage/IMEI do not match or verification on Rabbit Exchange App fails
  * Screen lock or icloud lock is not disabled.
  * Phone has damages on body (bends, dents, cracks, scratches, loose panel) or screen (discoloration, dead pixels, cracks, spots, lines, traces of replacement)

#####

Exchange tip

  * If old phone is rejected during pickup, you can pay the exchange discount amount at the time of delivery by card or cash and keep the new phone
  * The “Limited-Time Discount” will not be refunded if the old item is successfully picked up

##  10 days Service Centre Replacement

Replacement Reason  |  Replacement Period  |  Replacement Policy   
---|---|---  
Physical Damage,  
Wrong and Missing Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  Replacement   
Defective Item  |  10 days from delivery  |  iQOO warranty policy (at Service Centre)   
  
__

Defective item:

  * Amazon may provide support via self-help guides or on call or at doorstep, as applicable. 
  * If this issue is not resolved, please contact iQOO or visit the Service Centre.
  * iQOO will repair the product or provide a replacement or Defective certificate, as applicable. The time taken for resolution will be as per iQOO warranty policies.
  * Please check for nearest Brand service center in your location. For details [ click here ](https://www.amazon.in/gp/help/customer/display.html?ie=UTF8&nodeId=202064020)

  
Physical Damage, Wrong, Missing Items:

  * Returns will not be accepted if it is an Open Box Delivery order
  * Remote verification by image/video will be done by Amazon

upload an image for verification. Please visit the nearest iQOO Service Centre
for product-related issues. Further support will be provided by the brand at
their service centre as per their warranty policies.

and accessories. Unlock the device (screen lock, iCloud lock, etc.) and delete
your Google account for a successful pick-up.

[__How are ratings calculated?](javascript:void\(0\))

To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we
don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how
recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also
analyses reviews to verify trustworthiness.

### Customers say

Customers find the phone to be an excellent all-rounder with impressive
display quality that produces vibrant and clear photos, and appreciate its
top-notch performance with unmatched battery and charging speed. They consider
it good value for money. The heating and charging speed aspects receive mixed
feedback - while some report no heating issues and 40-minute full charge
times, others experience heating problems and slow charging. The camera
quality receives negative feedback from multiple customers.

##### [ _4.0 out of 5 stars_ My experience about the phone after 10 days of
buying it ](/gp/customer-reviews/RJTM6Y3UYPKB3/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8)

Reviewed in India on 5 August 2025

Colour: Inferno Red __Size: 12GB+256GB __Verified Purchase

1st Amazon should provide an open box delivery  
2nd I didn't like the box of the phone it looks very cheap quality compared to
the price of the phone even we get a better box and packaging in chepar
segment smartphone  
3rd phone is good as it's specifications it comes with Snapdragon 8s Gen 4 my
main reason of buying it was also the performance for Gaming ( BGMI )  
4th It can run BGMI 120FPS easily and it's 144 hz Display provide 144FPS
feature in Gaming Mode Specially the Monster Mode which is must to be on while
gaming and other features like Esports mode etc  
5th Camera is good as the phone is focused on performance centric it clicks
decent pictures and video's with his 50 MP Main camera and 8 MP Ultra wide
Camera  
6th Not a Fan of OneTouch OS on this phone the Software experience is not like
a Flagship but ok ok as a previous VIVO user the OS is Familiar so not a big
issue for me but if someone is shifting from some other brand they can feel a
downgrade in Software Experience  
7th phone has some bugs, Glitches and issues as it Comes with blotware Apps
which we have to delete and some AI image rendering glitch in albums and
Mainly the Heating issue of the phone While gaming it becomes so hot that i
can feel the heat in my hands while gaming but the good thing it doesn't
effect the gaming experience it runs smoothly  
I believe iQOO will fix these issues in the upcoming updates  
8th last but not the least as my own opinion or may be some other user's would
have also noticed that the Phone is polycarbonate Plastic built and it's very
easy to get scratches on your phone as a protection we use phone covers and
case to prevent it but when I use the phone cover provided in the box i
noticed that the cover is scratching my phone from the edges and I can see the
paint coming out so I have decided to leminate my phone i know that will
increase the heating but atleast my phone will be protected form the scratches
so I can get a better resell value in future  
  
.. thats my opinion on The iQOO Neo 10

#####  My experience about the phone after 10 days of buying it

  
Reviewed in India on 5 August 2025

1st Amazon should provide an open box delivery  
2nd I didn't like the box of the phone it looks very cheap quality compared to
the price of the phone even we get a better box and packaging in chepar
segment smartphone  
3rd phone is good as it's specifications it comes with Snapdragon 8s Gen 4 my
main reason of buying it was also the performance for Gaming ( BGMI )  
4th It can run BGMI 120FPS easily and it's 144 hz Display provide 144FPS
feature in Gaming Mode Specially the Monster Mode which is must to be on while
gaming and other features like Esports mode etc  
5th Camera is good as the phone is focused on performance centric it clicks
decent pictures and video's with his 50 MP Main camera and 8 MP Ultra wide
Camera  
6th Not a Fan of OneTouch OS on this phone the Software experience is not like
a Flagship but ok ok as a previous VIVO user the OS is Familiar so not a big
issue for me but if someone is shifting from some other brand they can feel a
downgrade in Software Experience  
7th phone has some bugs, Glitches and issues as it Comes with blotware Apps
which we have to delete and some AI image rendering glitch in albums and
Mainly the Heating issue of the phone While gaming it becomes so hot that i
can feel the heat in my hands while gaming but the good thing it doesn't
effect the gaming experience it runs smoothly  
I believe iQOO will fix these issues in the upcoming updates  
8th last but not the least as my own opinion or may be some other user's would
have also noticed that the Phone is polycarbonate Plastic built and it's very
easy to get scratches on your phone as a protection we use phone covers and
case to prevent it but when I use the phone cover provided in the box i
noticed that the cover is scratching my phone from the edges and I can see the
paint coming out so I have decided to leminate my phone i know that will
increase the heating but atleast my phone will be protected form the scratches
so I can get a better resell value in future  
  
.. thats my opinion on The iQOO Neo 10

#####  Front cameras waste.heating issue(games,camera)

  
Reviewed in India on 10 August 2025

Front camera worst even my old phone poco m2 pro which is I bought 13999 is
having best camera.main camera good.and battery not looks like 7000 mah it
looks like 6000 mah.battery fast charging very good with in 30 min
100%,display good.processor performance very good.gaming support 120 fps it
may increase up to 144fps..but battery drains fastly....while using camera and
playing games phone is heating...only main camera is good remain not
better.connectivity is good.. stereo speakers avarage.. overall performance
wise good phone..after using 20 days iam posting this.in lighting conditions
front camera avarage. Whatsapp video calling quality worst.My ratings camera
2.4/5,,battery 3.5/5,,display 4.5/5,, performance 5/5,, NFC ,IR BLASTER ,Q1
CHIP,IP 65 RATING,HDR SUPPORT, EVERYTHING HERE EXCEPT IP 69 RATING ,NO
TELEPHOTO LENCE IN CAMERAS...weight wise comfortable in handfeel.smooth
performance.build quality not better.OVERALL ABOUT THIS PHONE MY RATING
(3.5/5).
